#####

Old Phone will be rejected during pickup if

*   * Phone is not in working condition
  * RAM/Storage/IMEI do not match or verification on Rabbit Exchange App fails
  * Screen lock or icloud lock is not disabled.
  * Phone has damages on body (bends, dents, cracks, scratches, loose panel) or screen (discoloration, dead pixels, cracks, spots, lines, traces of replacement)

#####

Exchange tip

  * If old phone is rejected during pickup, you can pay the exchange discount amount at the time of delivery by card or cash and keep the new phone
  * The “Limited-Time Discount” will not be refunded if the old item is successfully picked up

##  10 days Service Centre Replacement

Replacement Reason  |  Replacement Period  |  Replacement Policy   
---|---|---  
Defective Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  OnePlus warranty policy (at Service Centre)   
Physical Damage,  
Wrong and Missing Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  Replacement   
  
__

Defective item:

  * Amazon may provide support via self-help guides or on call or at doorstep, as applicable. 
  * If this issue is not resolved, please contact OnePlus or visit the Service Centre.
  * OnePlus will repair the product or provide a replacement or Defective certificate, as applicable. The time taken for resolution will be as per OnePlus warranty policies.
  * Please check for nearest Brand service center in your location. For details [ click here ](https://www.amazon.in/gp/help/customer/display.html?ie=UTF8&nodeId=202064020)

  
Physical Damage, Wrong, Missing Items:

  * Returns will not be accepted if it is an Open Box Delivery order
  * Remote verification by image/video will be done by Amazon

#  About this item

  * Flagship Performance with Snapdragon(TM) 8s Gen 3: Couple this with the latest LPDDR5X RAM and segment-leading VC cooling (7300mm2), enjoy unprecedented 144 FPS BGMI and CODM steady-smooth gaming for a cool 5 hours. 
  * Flagship 50MP Front and Back Cameras Born for the Night: Best-in-class clarity and natural-looking colors for selfies, portraits, groufies and 4K 60 FPS videos. Perfection — front, back, night or light. 
  * Beast-mode 6800 mAh Battery + All-new Bypass Charging: Binge and game with up to 19.8 hrs of YouTube and 9.5 hrs of BGMI with our flagship-crushing battery. Bypass Charging powers the phone directly from the charger to keep temperatures low and frame rates high — a feature tailor-made for gaming. 
  * 144Hz 1.5K AMOLED Display with Aqua Touch 2.0: Enjoy flagship-killer smooth visuals and accurate touch response at up to 3000Hz, even with wet or oily fingers. Ideal for all-day use in the rain, morning, and night. 
  * Make Good Photos Great with AI: Nord 5 steals a full range of AIs from the OnePlus 13 — from AI Eraser, AI Detail Boost and AI Unblur that remove bystanders and turn off-focus images in-focus, to all-new AI Reframe that generates compositions for better framing, and AI Perfect Shot corrects blinked eyes and awkward faces in your groufies. 
  * Study Smarter with Dual AI – Google and OnePlus: Relax and let AI do the work for you. With AI Voice Scribe (transcribe, translate, and summarize Zoom/Google meetings, YouTube content etc), Circle to Search, Gemini Live (ask anything), and so much more. 
  * “Faster than 5G” Internet Speeds: With 5G-Advanced, the Nord 5 delivers up to 3 times the 5G data speeds. It conquers high-congestion zones like packed stadiums, concerts, crowded café environments effortlessly, allowing fast internet even with just 2 signal bars. 
  * Fast and Built to Last: Nord 5 ships with the latest (and smoothest) OxygenOS 15, promising 4 Android version upgrades plus 6 years of security updates. With our 6-year system smoothness guarantee and 4-year healthy battery promise, your phone stays fast and smooth for years to come.

[__How are ratings calculated?](javascript:void\(0\))

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we
don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how
recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also
analyses reviews to verify trustworthiness.

### Customers say

Customers find this phone to be an excellent mid-range device with sharp
camera quality and a butter-smooth UI experience. They appreciate its long
battery life, lasting up to 2 days with usage, and consider it good value for
money, particularly for mid-range buyers. The display receives positive
feedback, with one customer highlighting its 1.5K resolution, while the design
features a glossy matte finish. While some customers report no heating issues,
others mention heating problems.

 _5 out of 5 stars_

##### A real complete package in 30k.

Great device at first impression. Excellent processor,mind blowing
camera,outstanding OS and superb battery life including 80 watt adapter in-
box. It's a complete package phone which I purchased in 30k(2k card discount)
Each and everything included in-box even the back cover which deserve
appreciation. Note: I'm using one plus for the first time. Before I used
lenovo,redmi,realme,vivo and samsung respectively. So, as a long time android
user I care about optimisation and clean software experience. That's why I
chose one plus over other competitors (like iqoo and poco) which might give
better processor and storage type. All in all this phone is a complete package
which is the reason I chose one plus. I hope this beautiful device stay with
me for a long time, at least 8 years.

##### [ _5.0 out of 5 stars_ OnePlus Nord 5 – A Balanced Mid-Range Powerhouse
](/gp/customer-reviews/R3AK06GLDF5IBB/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

Reviewed in India on 28 July 2025

Colour: Phantom Grey __Size: 8GB+256GB __Verified Purchase

The OnePlus Nord 5 continues the brand’s legacy of delivering flagship-like
features at a competitive price. With a sleek, premium design and a vibrant
AMOLED display with 120Hz refresh rate, the device offers a smooth and
immersive viewing experience. Powered by the Snapdragon 7 Gen 3 chipset, it
handles multitasking, gaming, and daily tasks efficiently with minimal lag.  
  
Battery life is impressive, thanks to its 5000mAh battery and 80W SUPERVOOC
fast charging, which juices up the phone in under 40 minutes. The 50MP Sony
IMX890 main sensor captures detailed and color-rich photos, while the ultra-
wide and macro lenses are good for occasional use. The front camera delivers
crisp selfies, and 4K video recording adds value.  
  
OxygenOS remains clean and responsive.  
  
Overall, the OnePlus Nord 5 is an excellent choice who is seeking a reliable,
stylish, and powerful mid-range smartphone with great cameras and fast
charging.

shortlisted was Oppo Reno 14 that has same specs of One Plus 5. I settled for

##### [ _4.0 out of 5 stars_ A great mid ranger with few minor downgrades.
](/gp/customer-reviews/R3NTZDZNR3WD0P/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

Reviewed in India on 2 August 2025

Colour: Phantom Grey __Size: 12GB+512GB __Verified Purchase

Let me share a brief review about the Product,  
The OnePlus Nord 5 is overall a good Midrange phone, I love Oxygen OS UI very
smooth and responsive with no lags at all, Camera was not so Great when it
arrived yesterday, But today I got software update with July security patch
which fixes my camera significantly, currently camera is doing very decent job
10x Zoom is very usable considering it has no Periscope (Dedicated 2x or 3x
Zoom), The Mind Space feature do a basic UI related task, The AI in the image
editing is doing a great job. It has all the google AI (Gemini) and circle to
search feature, AI is doing a decent basic level job and need to improve. Live
Alerts (OnePlus dynamic island) doing a great job, but it is not supporting
3rd party music apps and it needs to work.  
Regarding Build Quality, Design and specs Build Quality is decent enough with
Plastic frame (It prevents device to heat up during heavy tasking/gaming but
might get scratches use phone case which is already provided in the box),,
Regarding Specs it has Qualcomm Snapdragon 8s Gen 3 processor which is one
year old but it is tried an tested, they can go with 8s Gen 4 or Dimensity
chipset which they provided in China, and they have given UFS 3.1 instead of
UFS 4.1, but that's not the big deal breaker for most of the consumers.  
  
Pros.  
1\. Great Software UI (No Lags at all)(4.5/5).  
2\. No Heating issue while using phone camera and multi tasking (4.5/5).  
3\. Great 1.5 K display with HDR Pro support (5/5).  
4\. Haptics are great.(4.5/5).  
5\. Camera is decent (3.5/5).  
6\. Software Update cycle (5/5)(4 Years of OS update and 6 years of security
patch).  
  
Cons:-  
1\. 80 W charger included (Last year 100 W charger was included with Oneplus
Nord 4)  
2\. Plastic Frame (Subjective).  
3\. UFS 3.1 storage instead of UFS 4.0/4.1(Subjective).  
4\. IP 65 rating only instead of IP68/69 rating.  
5\. Processor can be little better.  
  
Can charge 0 to 100 in 1h 10m (6800 mAh battery) which is decent.  
  
Overall I can give OnePlus Nord 5 a decent 3.7/5 stars, One can definitely buy
who wants premium level smooth OS, a decent camera and once who is casual to a
good level gamer., will add sample camera shots shortly.

Colour: Dry Ice __Size: 8GB+256GB __Verified Purchase

For 29ish K for the 8/256 model, you get  
  
* A really nice panel I must say. I really like the symmetrical edges on all sides. Makes this phone look a lot more beautiful and expensive than it really is. The panel is also smooth and bright, definitely the most standout feature for me  
  
* Okay back cameras. The main shooter is actually decent. The ultraWide captures very little detail most of the time. Safe to say, this phone is a one camera phone from the back.  
  
* Surprisingly sharp front camera. Really good  
  
* Performance, for me, is very good. I don't do any gaming above clash royale or push the phone very hard, and for that the performance is more than sufficient. But it should handle more demanding games as well  
  
* Battery life is really good. I am lasting 1.5 days easily and left with 30% with normal usage. Charging speed is good.  
  
* Speakers are okay. Not the best, not the worst. Atleast they are sterio  
  
* Feels good in the hand. The back finish feels nice. I got the sky blue color, looks very pretty. Feels more expensive than it is.  
  
* Extra features like lifetime green line warranty and 3 months extended warranty. AI feature set is really good.  
  
Cons: personally I liked the slider button better than the plus key.
Definitely would have liked to see a better ultrawide, or even a telephoto
cam. Nothing much else really. For 29K you get a good phone.  
  
Overall a decent device from a reputable company.
